<rating>1< /rating>< review>
We had an event here today, 2/9/2019, and it was possibly the worst experience using a venue that I've ever had. We booked over a month ago, but to our surprise, they double booked today with an hour overlap.
When we inquired about what was going on, the lady behind the counter literally said to us: "This isn't our fault and you'll just have to deal with it." They then took half of the space away from the other party to give it to us, which enraged the other party and caused them to be very belligerent towards us. We couldn't finish setting up until after when our party was supposed to start, and had to deal with both the staff and the previous party being extremely rude.
I would never book here again. Buyer beware.</review>

< text>
I was honored yesterday by my best friend of 40 years now treating me to lunch to celebrate my birthday. (We have known each other since we were ten years old and have been best buddies ever since.) We both had fish and chips which was outstanding! The serving of fish was so large that I took a box to take it and the remaining fries and onion rings home to eat for dinner. We could have ordered the smaller serving - the 'mini'- but we decided to go for it! Even with inflated prices everywhere due to COVID, the $20 it cost - including a Coke - was very reasonable considering the serving size and the quality of the dish. Our server was great too, and I liked the facility.<//text>

Loved the food. The tri tip with the chimichurri sauce was fenomenal. The tri tip comes with arugula bed and crumbles of goat cheese, I ordered it with “frings” (fries and onion rings) very tasty. The fish and chips was wonderful as well. The cod piece is a very generous serving and the dip sauces are wonderful. There is a curry flavor dip sauce that catches you by surprise in a good way!<//text>

<rating>4<//rating><Text>I always feel bad not giving 5 stars to a pretty good place but by definition 4 means I "Liked It" as opposed to "Loved It."  We liked the tri tip the most.  I also liked the juke box even though it is a dollar for most songs.  The lemonade tastes fresh so it is on the acidic/tart side.  Not sugary Minute Maid style.  I thought the fries were fairly typical thicker restaurant fries.  Nothing great or bad about them.  The onion rings were quite full of oil which is probably just a result of being "beer battered" but something to be aware of.  The fried chicken sandwich I had featured a peanut sauce on it that for me out flavored the rest of the sandwich.  If I ordered it again I would leave that off.  Finally we enjoyed the churro tower but the churros were on the crunchy side.  The service was pleasant, accurate, and brought lots of requested dipping sauces.  A good experience especially if you haven't tried it.<//Text>< pictures>

<Review>Everything you could ever do want from a Smart & Final can be found here. They are big on bulk, and big on savings. I was surprised at how large of a store this was. Not much produce selection, most of the fruit was old or sold. But they have anything you need to host a bbq or set up a taco stall.

The aisles were clean and organized. Lots of selection of different types of dog food. Tons of to-go containers and cleaning supplies. Frozen food isle was probably the biggest section of the store.

They have a full liquor corner, with top shelf selections. But you need assistance to access the area. Huge amounts of ready-to-drink beverages like monster energy, la croix and Starbucks Frappuccino’s.

Friendly store members. Free parking in the lot out front. Hard to notice this store from normal traffic, it’s a little tucked.< /Review><userid>106054869305142744230<//userid></record>

Worst plumbing experience. We just needed a simple shower cartridge change. We live in a condo so the HOA required a plumber to perform the work. We set the appt so that they could finish the work by 2 pm (and made them aware that the building was planning on turning the water back on at 2 pm). We called them several times because by ten last noon they still weren’t here. We live on te bottom floor so there was a lot of water built up in the line, so they decided to take the cartridge out of the shower and let it drain. During that time they left to go get a replacement part. In that time, gallons of water leaked into the wall behind the shower and soaked our brand new bedroom carpet, which shares a wall with the shower. We called the company, because the plumber was still gone getting the the replacement cartridge (mind you if he had let it drain, or instructed us to let the shower drain with the cartridge still in place, that water would not have drained into the wall behind the shower) and they told us they would send a restoration team, which they never did. All they did was vacuum our carpet (which did nothing, it’s 7 hours later and our carpet is still soaked). To top it all off, they charged us $321!!! We have a home warranty, and the warranty company had sent a previous company to do the job, but that company didn’t like having to work with an HOA (I’ll admit the water shut off process is annoying); that company quoted our home warranty $109 to perform the job, so that was all we got from our home warranty. I don’t understand why they charged us 3x what an other company had charged us. If they had been upfront w the cost, instead of telling us after they flooded our bedroom, we would have chosen another company, but instead I have a soggy bedroom and am out 200 bucks.<//review>

My sinks were backing up and I was in a panic! They began to overflow and to top it off I have family visiting from out of town! I spoke with a very a nice woman on the phone and let her know what was going on, she said she would put in as a priority and was very kind, courteous and professional. Within the hour Dan came and assessed the situation, very calm, quiet and knowledgeable. I never felt like I was being “bamboozled” as I have in the past. Being that I am a woman and the home owner I tend to feel like people will try to take advantage of the situation but this was not the case with Don. He was great!!

Only thing that irked me a little which had nothing to do with Don or his work is the fact that I have had Roto Rooter come to my home on different occasions within the last 5 years and every time is  the first time. They can’t ever seem to find my information from prior visits. I am a retired Air Force veteran and receive military discounts from this company and is much appreciated.... however why is it that the employees are not aware of this ??
